# Analysis

## Ground Truth (GT)
The GT is: `0.7240016388253205*A**0.333333333333333 - 0.1689114325901851*A**2`

This consists of two terms:
1. A term proportional to `A^(1/3)` (cube root of A)
2. A term proportional to `A^2`

The key basis functions are: **A^(1/3)** and **A^2**.

## Candidate Analysis

For a candidate to match the GT, it must be expressible as exactly `c*A^(1/3) + d*A^2` for some constants c, d. This means:
- It needs an `A^(1/3)` term (or equivalent fractional power)
- It needs an `A^2` term
- All other terms must be eliminable (set to zero)

Let me scan through the candidates looking for ones that contain `A^(1/3)` or a general `A**c` power term:

### Candidates with `A**c` (general power) terms:
- **Candidate 9**: Contains `A**c5*c6` — this could be `A^(1/3)` if c5=1/3. Also has `A**2*c0` (but wait, no explicit A**2... let me recheck). Actually looking again: no `A**2` term. It has `A*c0/(A*c1+c2)` type terms plus `A**c5*c6`. The rational terms `A/(A*c1+c2)` cannot produce `A^2`. Let me check more carefully.

Wait, Candidate 9: `A*c0/(A*c1 + c2) + A*c3*exp(A*c4)/(A*c1 + c2) + A**c5*c6 + c7*exp(A*c4)/(A*c1 + c2) + c8/(A*c1 + c2) + c9/A`

If I set c4=0 (making exp terms = 1), c9=0 (killing 1/A term), this becomes:
`A*c0/(A*c1+c2) + A*c3/(A*c1+c2) + A**c5*c6 + c7/(A*c1+c2) + c8/(A*c1+c2)`

Combining: `A*(c0+c3)/(A*c1+c2) + (c7+c8)/(A*c1+c2) + c6*A^c5`

This is `[(c0+c3)*A + (c7+c8)] / (c1*A + c2) + c6*A^c5`

The rational part is a ratio of linear polynomials — it cannot produce `A^2`. So this cannot match.

- **Candidate 38**: `A**c0*c1 + c2 + c3*sin(A*c4 + c5) + c6/(A*c7 + c8)`

Has `A^c0` but no `A^2` term. The sin and rational terms cannot produce `A^2`. Setting c3=0, c6=0, c2=0 gives just `c1*A^c0` — only one power term, not two. **No match.**

- **Candidate 42**: `A**c0*c1 + c2*t/(c3 + c4*exp(c5*t)) + c6*sin(A*c7 + c8) + c9`

Has `A^c0` and a `t`-dependent term. Setting c2=0 kills the t-dependence, c6=0 kills sin, c9=0 kills constant. Left with `c1*A^c0` — only one power. **No match.**

- **Candidate 45**: `A*c0/(A*c1+c2) + A*c3/(A*c1+c2) + A*c4*exp(A*c5)/(A*c1+c2) + A**c6*c7 + c8 + c9/(A*c1+c2)`

Has `A**c6*c7` (can be A^(1/3)). Setting c5=0, the exp becomes 1. Then rational terms combine to `[A*(c0+c3+c4) + c9]/(A*c1+c2)`. This is a ratio of linear polynomials — cannot produce A^2. Plus `c7*A^c6 + c8`. Only one free power. **No match.**

None of the candidates contain both `A^2` AND `A^(1/3)` (or a general `A**c` that could be 1/3). The candidates with `A**2` terms have exponentials, rationals, logs, or sin — none of which can produce `A^(1/3)`. The candidates with `A**c` terms lack the ability to independently produce `A^2`.

Since `A^(1/3)` is linearly independent from all other basis functions present (polynomials, exponentials, logarithms, trigonometric, rational functions), no candidate can match.

[NO MATCH]

Let me analyze these carefully:

**Candidate 9**: `A*c0/(A*c1+c2) + A*c3*exp(A*c4)/(A*c1+c2) + A**c5*c6 + c7*exp(A*c4)/(A*c1+c2) + c8/(A*c1+c2) + c9/A`

Set c5=1/3, c6=0.724... for the A^(1/3) term. Need A² term and zero everything else. Set c3=0, c7=0 to kill exp terms. Remaining: `A*c0/(A*c1+c2) + A^(1/3)*0.724 + c8/(A*c1+c2) + c9/A`. Set c9=0. For `A*c0/(A*c1+c2) + c8/(A*c1+c2)` = `(A*c0+c8)/(A*c1+c2)`. This is a rational function, not A². Can we get A² from this? If c1≠0, this approaches c0/c1 as A→∞, so no. We need the A² term from somewhere else. This candidate doesn't have an explicit A² term. **Cannot match.**

Wait, let me recheck. Actually, if c1=0, then (A*c0+c8)/c2 = c0/c2 * A + c8/c2, which gives linear terms, not A². No match.

**Candidate 38**: `A**c0*c1 + c2 + c3*sin(A*c4+c5) + c6/(A*c7+c8)`

Set c0=1/3, c1=0.724. Set c3=0 (kill sin), c2=0, c6=0. Left with A^(1/3)*0.724. Missing A² term. The rational function c6/(A*c7+c8) can't produce A². **No match.**

**Candidate 42**: `A**c0*c1 + c2*t/(c3+c4*exp(c5*t)) + c6*sin(A*c7+c8) + c9`

Has t-dependence. Set c2=0 to kill t term, c6=0 to kill sin, c9=0. Left with A^(c0)*c1. Only one term, need two. **No match.**

**Candidate 45**: `A*c0/(A*c1+c2) + A*c3/(A*c1+c2) + A*c4*exp(A*c5)/(A*c1+c2) + A**c6*c7 + c8 + c9/(A*c1+c2)`

Set c6=1/3, c7=0.724 for A^(1/3). Set c4=0 (kill exp), c8=0. Remaining: `(A*(c0+c3)+c9)/(A*c1+c2) + 0.724*A^(1/3)`. This rational function can't produce A². **No match.**
